GT: -c0*sqrt(A) + c1*_w*cos(log(A + c2))
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed function (no dependence on `t`):
\[
f(A)= -0.2596955894\,\sqrt{A} + 0.9122976147\,\cos(\log(A+1)).
\]
So any matching candidate must (i) be independent of `t` after parameter choice, and (ii) be able to represent simultaneously a \(\sqrt{A}\) term and a \(\cos(\log(A+1))\) term (with the correct shift “+1” inside the log), with no extra functional forms left over.

Also can set \(c7=1\) to get \(\log(|A|+1)\) and for \(A\ge 0\), \(|A|=A\). However GT uses \(\sqrt{A}\) (not \(|A|\) or powers available here except via exp term), and candidate has only polynomial terms \(A^2, A\) plus exp(A*const) and trig-log. There is **no way to produce \(\sqrt{A}\)** from these components for all \(A\). Cannot.

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK9)
============================================================
GT: -c0*sqrt(A) + c1*_w*cos(log(A + c2))
Candidates evaluated: 50
Matched candidate IDs: []
Matched candidates: []

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the ground truth:

**GT:** `-0.2597*sqrt(A) + 0.9123*cos(log(A + 1))`

This expression has two key basis functions:
1. `sqrt(A)` — a square root term
2. `cos(log(A + 1))` — a cosine of logarithm term

Let me analyze each candidate for the presence of these basis functions.

**Key observations about GT:**
- No dependence on `t` (time-independent)
- Contains `sqrt(A)` which is `A^0.5`
- Contains `cos(log(A+1))` — a transcendental oscillatory function of A
- No polynomial terms in A (no A², A, or constant terms unless they come from the cos/sqrt)

For a candidate to match, it must be able to produce both `sqrt(A)` and `cos(log(A+1))` terms, and all other terms must be eliminable (set to zero).

Let me go through each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** Rational functions of A with `A^c3` terms. No cos, no log. Cannot produce `cos(log(A+1))`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 2:** Polynomial + rational in A. No transcendental functions. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 3:** `A²c0 + Ac1 + c2*tanh(c3*t+c4) + c5*exp(c6*t)`. Has tanh and exp of t, no cos(log). Even setting t-dependent terms to zero (c2=0, c5=0), left with polynomial in A. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 4:** `A²c0 + Ac1 + Ac2/(A+c3) + c4*|A| + c5`. Rational/polynomial. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 5:** `A²c0 + Ac1 + c2 + c3*exp(Ac4) + c5*sin(c6*log(c7*|A|+1) + c8)`

Set c0=0, c1=0, c2=0, c3=0 (or c4=0 to make exp=1 and absorb into c2). Then we have:
`c5*sin(c6*log(c7*|A|+1) + c8)`

With A≥0, |A|=A. Setting c7=1, c6=1, c8=π/2: `c5*sin(log(A+1) + π/2) = c5*cos(log(A+1))`. That gives the cos(log(A+1)) term. ✓

But we also need `-0.2597*sqrt(A)`. The remaining terms are `A²c0 + Ac1 + c2 + c3*exp(Ac4)`. None of these can produce `sqrt(A)`. Setting c3*exp(Ac4): this is an exponential, not sqrt. **NO MATCH**

Wait — let me reconsider. We need BOTH sqrt(A) AND cos(log(A+1)). Candidate 5 can produce cos(log(A+1)) but not sqrt(A). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 6-24:** These are polynomials, rationals, exponentials in A or t, or combinations. None contain both sqrt(A) and cos(log(A+1)). **NO MATCH** for all.

**Candidate 28:** `c0*tanh(c1*t+c2) + c3*cos(c4*log(c5*|A|+1)) + c6*|A|^c7/(c8+|A|^c7)`

Set c0=0 (eliminate tanh/t-dependence). With A≥0: `c3*cos(c4*log(c5*A+1)) + c6*A^c7/(c8+A^c7)`

Set c4=1, c5=1: `c3*cos(log(A+1))` ✓

For the second term: `c6*A^c7/(c8+A^c7)`. Can this equal `-0.2597*sqrt(A)`? This is `A^c7` divided by `(c8+A^c7)`, a sigmoid-like function. For it to equal `sqrt(A)` for all A≥0, we'd need `c6*A^c7 = sqrt(A)*(c8+A^c7)`, which gives `c6*A^c7 = c8*sqrt(A) + A^(c7+0.5)`. This can't hold for all A. **NO MATCH**

**Candidates 29, 31, 33, 37, 43, 45:** These contain `A^c` terms. Setting c to 0.5 gives sqrt(A), but none also have cos(log(A+1)). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 27:** `A²c0 + A^c1*c2 + c3*tanh(c4*t+c5) + c6*exp(c7*t)*log(Ac8+1)`. Has log but not cos(log). **NO MATCH**

After checking all 50 candidates, none can simultaneously produce both `sqrt(A)` and `cos(log(A+1))`.

Candidate 1 through 50 verdict: [NO MATCH] for all.

Matched candidate IDs: []

[NO MATCH]

Conclusion: No match
